                function addOnload(a) {
                    if ('undefined' != typeof(window.attachEvent)) {
                        return window.attachEvent('onload', a);
                    } else {
                        if (window.addEventListener) {
                            return window.addEventListener('load', a, false);
                        }
                    }
                }
                // Loads the script using vanilla Javascript given a url 26/Aug/2016
               function scriptOnload(src) {
                   addOnload(function () {
                       var s = document.createElement('script');
                       s.src = src;
                       s.async = true;
                       document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0].appendChild(s);
                   });
               }

    /** 
    * JOBS-8805
    * Local storage cache bursting
    * 
    * @author john.lukose@quikr.com
    */
    
    // Function (IIFE) to perform localstorage cache bursting
    (function (localStorageCacheBurstingDetails) {
        JobSnow.localStorageCacheBurstingDetails = localStorageCacheBurstingDetails;
        
        if(window.localStorage && 1 === parseInt(localStorageCacheBurstingDetails.featureEnabled)) {
            try {
                var previousLocalStorageVersion       = window.localStorage.jobsLocalStorageVersion || 0;
                var previousGlobalLocalStorageVersion = window.localStorage.jobsGlobalLocalStorageVersion || 0;
                var reloadPage = false;

                var localStorageKeys = [];
                for (var key in localStorage) {
                    if (localStorage.hasOwnProperty(key)) { 
                        localStorageKeys.push(key);
                    }
                }

                // Specific cache bursting
                if(parseInt(localStorageCacheBurstingDetails.jobsLocalStorageVersion) > parseInt(previousLocalStorageVersion)) {
                    var storage = localStorageCacheBurstingDetails.storage;

                    for (var key in storage) {
                        if (storage.hasOwnProperty(key)) {

                            if(!storage[key].startsWith('reg-')) {
                                // direct remove
                                localStorage.removeItem(storage[key]);
                                reloadPage = true;
                            } else {
                                storage[key] = storage[key].replace('reg-', '');
                                // regex remove
                                for (var key1 in localStorageKeys) {
                                    if(RegExp(storage[key]).test(localStorageKeys[key1])) {
                                        localStorage.removeItem(localStorageKeys[key1]);
                                        reloadPage = true;
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }

                // Entire cache bursting
                if(parseInt(localStorageCacheBurstingDetails.jobsGlobalLocalStorageVersion) > parseInt(previousGlobalLocalStorageVersion)) {
                    localStorage.clear();
                    reloadPage = true;
                }

                // Updating cache version
                window.localStorage.jobsLocalStorageVersion = localStorageCacheBurstingDetails.jobsLocalStorageVersion;
                window.localStorage.jobsGlobalLocalStorageVersion = localStorageCacheBurstingDetails.jobsGlobalLocalStorageVersion;

                // Reload page
                if(reloadPage)
                    location.reload();

            } catch (e) {
                console.log('Exception occured while localstorage cache bursting', e);
            }
        }
    })({"featureEnabled":1,"jobsLocalStorageVersion":9,"jobsGlobalLocalStorageVersion":1,"storage":["roleSubRoleOptions"],"featureEnabledPWA":1,"jobsLocalStorageVersionPWA":9,"jobsGlobalLocalStorageVersionPWA":0,"storagePWA":["roleSubRoleOptions"],"info":"increase the version to perform localstorage cache burst"});
    // End : JOBS-8805

        var expires = "expires="+ curr_date.toUTCString();
        document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + ";" + expires; //setting cookie value
    }
